<NOTE>
If what follows appears as gobbledygook on your screen, you have to select all and change the font to a Japanese font. In some  wordprocessing programs (such as Nisus or Solowriter on the Macintosh) you have to force the font change (in case of Nisus by pressing the  Shift key while selecting the font from the Font menu).
</NOTE>
</NOTESSTMT>
<SOURCEDESC>
<BIBL>Contains the three indexes of the Bukkyo daijiten 佛教大辞典. Mochizuki Shinko 望月信亨 and Tsukamoto Zenryu 塚本善隆, eds. Sekai seiten kankokai 世界聖典刊行会, 10 vols., Tokyo 1959-1963 (third ed., revised and expanded 増訂版).
The three indexes are as follows:
1. In vol. 7, index to vols. 1-6, 41'800 entries.
2. In vol. 8, index to vol. 8, 2'961 entries.
3. In vol. 10, index to vols. 9-10, 5'563 entries.
Errata list in vol. 8, pp. 1-11. This list deletes 9 entries included in previous indexes.

N.B. 1: Since page numbers are redundant, the volumes concerned are indicated for each entry.
N.B. 2: Each line is constituted of three fields separated by tabs: 1. Entry in kanjis 2. Volumes concerned 3. Page number. Readings between brackets 【→...】 are indications that there is another entry under a different reading. Asterisks * indicate that the word itself is the subject of the article.
</BIBL>
</SOURCEDESC>
</FILEDESC>
